- [TomWright/dasel](https://github.com/TomWright/dasel) - Select, put and delete data from JSON, TOML, YAML, XML and CSV files with a single tool. Supports conversion between formats and can be used as a Go package. (⭐️ 7607)
- [mikefarah/yq](https://github.com/mikefarah/yq) - yq is a portable command-line YAML, JSON, XML, CSV, TOML  and properties processor (⭐️ 14087)
- [tdewolff/minify](https://github.com/tdewolff/minify) - Go minifiers for web formats (⭐️ 3967)

## zig 

- [lightpanda-io/zig-js-runtime](https://github.com/lightpanda-io/zig-js-runtime) - Add a JS runtime in your Zig project (⭐️ 183)
- [lightpanda-io/browser](https://github.com/lightpanda-io/browser) - Lightpanda: the headless browser designed for AI and automation (⭐️ 9715)
- [oven-sh/bun](https://github.com/oven-sh/bun) - Incredibly fast JavaScript runtime, bundler, test runner, and package manager – all in one (⭐️ 80404)
- [zigtools/zls](https://github.com/zigtools/zls) - A language server for Zig supporting developers with features like autocomplete and goto definition (⭐️ 4162)
- [jiacai2050/zig-curl](https://github.com/jiacai2050/zig-curl) - Zig bindings for libcurl (⭐️ 124)
- [extism/extism](https://github.com/extism/extism) - The framework for building with WebAssembly (wasm). Easily & securely load wasm modules, move data, call functions, and build extensible apps. (⭐️ 5183)
